The toilet has a strong smell after the exhaust is turned on, but the smell is lighter when it is not turned on. The smell of this toilet is very discounted. I didn't sleep well at night, maybe I am more attached to the bed.
The advantage is that the hotel is right next to the entrance of Guoqing Temple, which is very convenient. There are plenty of parking spaces. There is a 1.5-hour explanation of Guoqing Temple at 8:30 in the morning (with Bluetooth, the lady's explanation is also very good). Let's talk about it separately. Remember to go to the legal circulation office of Guoqing Temple. Get a bracelet, incense bag, and lucky cat pendant. They are all beautiful and the price is very affordable. The hotel has Yijinjing training and meditation in the evening, and copying scriptures in the afternoon, which are all good. There is also Xide Coffee next door, which is very convenient and close to Sanmu and Food. On rainy days, there are umbrellas in the hotel room. The breakfast is average, there are only two breakfasts, and children over 120 have to pay 48 yuan. Dinner is more than 100 yuan per person, and it is okay according to the first few dishes on Dianping.
I gave the children two postcards when I left, and the children were very happy.
